## How to Fix

### Missing Files
- Verify the file exists at the specified path
- Check for typos in the import path
- Ensure the file wasn't moved or deleted
- Update path aliases in tsconfig.json if needed

### Missing Exports
- Verify the symbol is exported from the target file
- Check for typos in the import statement
- Ensure the export wasn't removed or renamed
- Use named exports explicitly if importing from a barrel file

### Auto-Fix
To automatically fix broken imports:
```bash
node import-resolver.mjs         # Dry run (preview)
DRY_RUN=false node import-resolver.mjs  # Apply fixes
```

---
*External packages (npm, etc.) are assumed valid if installed.*
